2.1.1 Tastatur (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.1.1 (2.1.1 - Nivå A)
SERIOUS

Interactive input has tabindex='-1' - not keyboard accessible

<input aria-hidden="true" class="shCc15" tabindex="-1" type="submit" value="Søk"/>
Remove tabindex='-1' unless element is in an inactive state
2.4.1 Hopp over blokker (1 avvik)
Testregel 2.4.1 (2.4.1 - Nivå A)
MODERATE

Page has no skip link to bypass navigation

<body>
Add a skip link at the start of the page: <a href='#main'>Hopp til hovedinnhold</a>

Testregel 1.2.2 (1.2.2 - Nivå A)
CRITICAL

<a class="xfxJ27 wixui-vertical-menu__item-label" data-testid="linkElement" href="https://www.elklagenemnda.no/_files/ugd/74c3c7_d4ed748bfd8e4ab9aa76b31050aeb0ed.pdf" target="_blank">Vedtekter</a>

2.1.1 Tastatur (1 avvik)

SERIOUS

Interactive input has tabindex='-1' - not keyboard accessible
